Joe Biden, Earth politician from the pre-interstellar backwater Sol-III, has accumulated zero criminal convictions, zero successful impeachments, and precisely one (1) parking ticket in Wilmington, Delaware, circa 1978—paid in full, because even Galactic Vogon bureaucracy respects prompt fine payment when the alternative is a complimentary ear-reaming.
